%META:TOPICINFO{author="RobertEngel" date="1314659411" format="1.1" reprev="1.160" version="1.160"}%
---+!! %WIKITOOLNAME% Site-Level Preferences

This topic defines __site-level__ settings that apply to all users and webs on this TWikiSite.

__%X% Note:__ This topic should be regarded as read-only, so that upgrades can safely overwrite it without risk to your customizations.

Preference settings local to your site should be set in [[%LOCALSITEPREFS%]] (this topic is pointed to by {LocalSitePreferences}, which is set by the admin in the =configure= interface). Settings in [[%LOCALSITEPREFS%]] will override settings in this topic, and should be used for defining custom settings and variables.

[[TWikiVariables#PreferencesVariables][Read more]] on how to set Preferences Variables.

%EDITPREFERENCES{"TWikiPreferencesForm"}% _(Click for form-based editing of existing preferences.)_ 
%TOC%

#DefaultWebPreferences
---++ Default Web Preferences

%X% *NOTE:* These are just defaults; don't change them here. Instead, add them to the !WebPreferences topic in each web

   * List of selected topics in a web (used in menus) 
      * Set WEBTOPICLIST = [[WebChanges][Changes]] %SEP% [[WebIndex][Index]] %SEP% [[WebSearch][Search]] %SEP% Go <input type="text" name="topic" size="16" />    

   * Web-specific background color: (is overwritten by web preferences) 
      * Set WEBBGCOLOR = #FFD8AA    

   * [[http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Favicon][favicon]]: Attach a =favicon.ico= to a web's WebPreferences or add a =FAVICON= setting to WebPreferences 
      * Set FAVICON = %PUBURLPATH%/%BASEWEB%/%WEBPREFSTOPIC%/favicon.ico    

   * Image, URL and alternate tooltip text of web's logo. 
      * Set WEBLOGOIMG = %WIKILOGOIMG%    
      * Set WEBLOGOURL = %WIKILOGOURL%    
      * Set WEBLOGOALT = %WIKILOGOALT%    

   * List this web in the %TWIKIWEB%.SiteMap: 
      * If yes, set SITEMAPLIST to =on=, do not set NOSEARCHALL, and add the "what" and "use to..." description for the site map. Make sure to list only links that include the name of the web, e.g. %WEB%.Topic links. 
      * Set SITEMAPLIST = on    
      * Set SITEMAPWHAT = Describe what this web does.    
      * Set SITEMAPUSETO = ...to do something.    

   * Copyright notice: 
      * Set WEBCOPYRIGHT = <span class="twikiRight"> <a href="http://twiki.org/"><img src="%PUBURLPATH%/%TWIKIWEB%/TWikiLogos/T-logo-80x15.gif" alt="This site is powered by the TWiki collaboration platform" width="80" height="15" title="This site is powered by the TWiki collaboration platform" border="0" /></a></span>%MAKETEXT{"Copyright &Â© by the contributing authors. All material on this collaboration platform is the property of the contributing authors." args="1999-%GMTIME{$year}%"}% <br /> Ideas, requests, problems regarding this page? <a href='https://ticket.grid.iu.edu/goc/twiki'>Send feedback</a>.

   * Simplified Copyright notice for the WebRss feed (don't use any special characters, html tags, entities, wiki markup or WikiWords) 
      * Set WEBRSSCOPYRIGHT = Copyright %GMTIME{"$year"}% by contributing authors    

   * Exclude web from a =web="all"= search: (Set to =on= for hidden webs; is overwritten by web preferences) __Note__ it is much better to use TWikiAccessControls in individual webs to control who can and can't view the contents of a web. NOSEARCHALL is retained for compatibility, but you should avoid using it. 
      * Set NOSEARCHALL =     
   * Prevent automatic linking of [[%TWIKIWEB%.WikiWords][WikiWords]] and acronyms (if set to =on=); link WikiWords (if empty); can be overwritten by web preferences: 
      * Set NOAUTOLINK = 
      * __Note:__ Use the =[[...][...]]= syntax to link topics in case you disabled WikiWord linking. The =...= syntax can be used to prevents links within a block of text. 

   * Warn if =%INCLUDE{}%= of topic fails: Fail silently if empty or =off=. Output warning message (defined in templates/oopsalerts.tmpl) if set to =on=. Otherwise output specific text (use =$topic= for topic). You can override this in web preferences, or by using a =warn="..."= parameter with =%INCLUDE{}%= : 
      * Set INCLUDEWARNING = on    

---++ Default User Settings

%X% *NOTE:* They are typically redefined in topics of individual %MAINWEB%.TWikiUsers

   * Show tool-tip topic info on mouse-over of WikiWord links. Setting can be on, off, or customized. An empty setting or off setting disables the tool-tips (for better performance). The setting can contain $summary to show the topic summary, $date for the last change date, $rev for the revision, $username for the login name of the last editor, $wikiname for the WikiName, $wikiusername for %MAINWEB%.WikiName, $topic for the topic name, and $web for the web name 
      * Set LINKTOOLTIPINFO = off    
      * #Set LINKTOOLTIPINFO = $username - $date - $rev: $summary 

   * Some skins have two editors available; the default editor, and a second editor which is usually a WYSIWYG editor (the second editor is used by hitting the %MAKETEXT{"WYSIWYG"}% link in =pattern= or =classic= skins). If COMPOSER is not set, the second editor will work the same as the _default_ editor. If the !WysiwygPlugin is installed and it is set to 'kupu' (the default), then the *Kupu* WYSIWYG editor will be enabled. You can change the setting to use any editor that is enabled by setting the =cover= parameter on the edit URL. 
      * Set COMPOSER = kupu    

   * Horizontal size of text edit box: (can be overwritten by user preferences) 
      * Set EDITBOXWIDTH = 70    

   * Vertical size of text edit box: (can be overwritten by user preferences) 
      * Set EDITBOXHEIGHT = 22    

   * Style of text edit box. Set to =width: 99%= for full window width (default; this will overwrite the EDITBOXWIDTH setting), or =width: auto= to disable. This setting works for IE and some other recent browsers. (can be overwritten by user preferences) 
      * Set EDITBOXSTYLE = width: 99%    

   * Default state of the __Force New Revision__ (ForceNewRevision) check box in preview. Check box is initially checked if =Set FORCENEWREVISIONCHECKBOX = checked="checked"=, or unchecked if empty: (can be overwritten by user preferences) 
      * Set FORCENEWREVISIONCHECKBOX =     

   * Default state of the __Minor Changes, Don't Notify__ (DontNotify) check box in preview. Check box is initially checked if =Set DONTNOTIFYCHECKBOX = checked="checked"=, or unchecked if empty: (can be overwritten by user preferences) 
      * Set DONTNOTIFYCHECKBOX =     

   * Default state of the __link__ check box in the attach file page. Checkbox is initially checked if =Set ATTACHLINKBOX = checked="checked"=, or unchecked if empty ( =Set ATTACHLINKBOX ==). If checked, a link is created to the attached file at the end of the topic: (can be overwritten by user preferences) 
      * Set ATTACHLINKBOX =     

   * Format of file link when the __link__ check box is checked: (can be overwritten by user preferences) 
      * %H% *NOTE:* Keyword ==$name== gets expanded to filename; ==$comment== to comment; ==\t== to tab (3 spaces for bullets). <!-- verbatim tag required to prevent error in Apache log; does not suppress Set --> <verbatim>
      * Set ATTACHEDFILELINKFORMAT = \n   * [[%ATTACHURL%/$name][$name]]: $comment
</verbatim> 

   * Format of images when the __link__ check box is checked: (can be overwritten by user preferences) 
      * %H% *NOTE:* Keyword ==$name== gets expanded to filename; ==$comment== to comment; ==$size== to ==width="..." height="..."== attribute of ==img== tag; ==\t== to tab and ==\n== to linefeed (3 spaces for bullets). 
      * Set ATTACHEDIMAGEFORMAT = \n   * $comment: <br />\n     <img src="%ATTACHURLPATH%/$name" alt="$name" $size />    

---++ TWiki Platform Settings

   * TWiki site name: 
      * Set WIKITOOLNAME = TWiki    

   * Image, URL and alternate tooltip text of the logo *for this installation*: you should change these settings for your site, or they can be overwridden in !WebPreferences for individual webs by defining these variables there. 
      * Set WIKILOGOIMG = %PUBURL%/%TWIKIWEB%/TWikiLogos/T-logo-140x40-t.gif    
      * Set WIKILOGOURL = http://TWiki.org/    
      * Set WIKILOGOALT = Powered by %WIKITOOLNAME%    

   * Home page of this site 
      * Set WIKIHOMEURL = %SCRIPTURLPATH{"view"}%    

   * List of %WIKITOOLNAME% webs - on the first line of the upper toolbar (to add a new web, see ManagingWebs and %TWIKIWEB%.SiteMap): 
      * Set WIKIWEBLIST = [[%MAINWEB%.%HOMETOPIC%][%MAINWEB%]] %SEP% [[%TWIKIWEB%.%HOMETOPIC%][%TWIKIWEB%]] %SEP% [[Sandbox.%HOMETOPIC%][Sandbox]]    
      * %T% *NOTE:* To automatically list all non-hidden webs in alphabetical order, use the =%WEBLIST{}%= variable instead: <br /> %WEBLIST{"[[$name.%HOMETOPIC%][$name]]" separator=" | "}% 

   * Maximum size of %TWIKIWEB%.FileAttachments in KB, 0 for no limit: 
      * Set ATTACHFILESIZELIMIT = 10000    

   * Broadcast message for skins supporting a %BROADCASTMESSAGE% at the top of the page: (IMPORTANT: Set to empty message if not used; #Comment out unused messages) 
      * Set BROADCASTMESSAGE =     
      * #Set BROADCASTMESSAGE = <table width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="3" border="0"><tbody><tr><td bgcolor="yellow">%RED% *NOTE:* %ENDCOLOR% Edit and Attach will be disabled today between 05:00 PM and 06:00 PM PDT (00:00 to 01:00 GMT) for a scheduled %WIKITOOLNAME% maintenance. </td></tr></tbody></table> 
      * If you use PatternSkin: 
      * #Set BROADCASTMESSAGE = <p> *NOTE:* Edit and Attach will be disabled today between 05:00 PM and 06:00 PM PDT (00:00 to 01:00 GMT) for a scheduled %WIKITOOLNAME% maintenance.</p> 

   * Users or groups allowed to [[%TWIKIWEB%.ManagingWebs][create new webs]]: (ex: %MAINWEB%.TWikiAdminGroup) 
   * *This has been disabled for the TWiki-4.0.0 release due to a potential security hole - you must be in the TWikiAdminGroup to create a web* 
      * Set ALLOWWEBMANAGE = %MAINWEB%.TWikiAdminGroup    

---+++ Search Settings

   * Default type for search, one of: keyword (for search engine like syntax), regex (for RegularExpression search), or literal (for verbatim search) 
      * Set SEARCHDEFAULTTTYPE = keyword    
   * Default for =%SEARCH{}%= variable, one of: keyword, regex, or literal 
      * Set SEARCHVARDEFAULTTYPE = literal    
   * Stop words, e.g., common words and characters to exclude from a keyword search: 
      * Set SEARCHSTOPWORDS = a, all, am, an, and, any, as, at, b, be, by, c, d, e, for, from, g, h, how, i, i'm, i.e., in, is, isn't, it, it's, its, j, k, l, m, n, o, of, on, or, p, q, r, s, t, that, that's, the, this, to, u, v, w, was, wasn't, what, what's, when, where, who, who's, will, with, x, y, z    

---+++ E-mail Settings

   * TWiki administrator e-mail address: 
      * Set WIKIWEBMASTER = osg-twiki@opensciencegrid.org 

   * TWiki administrator name (first name and last name, e.g. =Fred Smith=): 
      * Set WIKIWEBMASTERNAME = TWiki Administrator    

   * 'Mail this topic' mailto: link - can be included in topics, templates or skins 
      * Set MAILTHISTOPIC = <a href="mailto:?subject=%BASETOPIC%&body=%TOPICURL%">%MAILTHISTOPICTEXT%</a>    

   * 'Mail this topic' link text 
      * Set MAILTHISTOPICTEXT = Send a link to this page    

   * URL for current topic 
      * Set TOPICURL = %SCRIPTURL{"view"}%/%WEB%/%BASETOPIC%    

---+++ HTTP-EQUIV Settings

   * %T% *NOTE:* Changing cache behaviour with these settings should not be necessary and may cause cache-related problems (e.g. TWiki:Codev.BackFromPreviewLosesText or TWiki:Codev.RefreshEditPage). These settings do not affect proxy caches. 
   * *NOTE:* The current values of these preferences are not displayed in view mode (values are <link>-tags). 

   * ==http-equiv== meta tags for ==view==, ==rdiff==, ==attach==, ==search*== scripts: 
      * #Set HTTP_EQUIV_ON_VIEW = 
      * Set HTTP_EQUIV_ON_VIEW = <link rel="alternate" type="application/rss+xml" title="RSS Feed" href="%SCRIPTURLPATH{"view"}%/%WEB%/WebRss" />    

   * ==http-equiv== meta tags for ==edit== script: 
      * Set HTTP_EQUIV_ON_EDIT =     

   * ==http-equiv== meta tags for ==preview== script: 
      * Set HTTP_EQUIV_ON_PREVIEW =

   * __Note:__ See TWikiSkinBrowser for currently installed skins

   * Custom overriding styles (enabled pr. default but empty, to prevent browsers from fetching %USERLAYOUTURL%-style URLs) 
      * Set USERLAYOUTURL =     
      * Set USERSTYLEURL =     
      * Set USERCOLORSURL =     

   * *PatternSkin header settings* 
      * Set WEBHEADERART = %PUBURLPATH%/%TWIKIWEB%/PatternSkin/TWiki_header.gif

---+++ Skin icons

   * Topic containing the icon graphics library. Icons can easily be rendered with =%ICON{name}%=.

---+++ Legacy support
   * Support for legacy "EDITTOPIC", used to be hard-coded, now replaced by TMPL:P conditional instantiation 
      * Set EDITURL = %SCRIPTURLPATH{"edit"}%/%WEB%/%TOPIC%?t=%GMTIME{"$epoch"}%    
      * Set EDITTOPIC = <a href="%EDITURL%" title="Edit Topic - deprecated usage - please see release notes">Edit</a>    

---++ Plugins Settings

   * You can enable/disable Plugins using the [[%SCRIPTURLPATH{"configure"}%][configure]] interface. 
   * Currently activated Plugins: %ACTIVATEDPLUGINS% 
   * %T% *NOTE:* You can enable/disable Plugins by passing a comma-separated list of Plugin names in the =debugenableplugins= url parameter; for example, %SCRIPTURL{"view"}%/%WEB%/%TOPIC%?debugenableplugins=SmiliesPlugin will display this topic with all Plugins disabled except the SmiliesPlugin. 
   * Detailed diagnostics can be found in InstalledPlugins 
   * Legacy settings: 
      * Set DISABLEDPLUGINS = The DISABLEDPLUGINS variable is no longer supported    
      * Set INSTALLEDPLUGINS = The INSTALLEDPLUGINS variable is no longer supported. You can set the Plugins execution order using the [[%SCRIPTURLPATH{"configure"}%][configure]] interface.

#ColorDefinitions
   * Colored text: (see more StandardColors) 
| You type: | =%RED% red text %ENDCOLOR% and %GREEN% green text %ENDCOLOR%= |
| You get: | %RED% red text %ENDCOLOR% and %GREEN% green text %ENDCOLOR% |
   * 
      * __Note:__ =%<color>%= text must end with =%ENDCOLOR%=. If you want to switch from one color to another one you first need to end the active color with =%ENDCOLOR%=, e.g. write =%RED% some text %ENDCOLOR% %GREEN% more text %ENDCOLOR%=. <!-- Two sets of colors follow: Color test and color setting --> 
      * %YELLOW% *Set YELLOW = looks like this* %ENDCOLOR% 
      * %ORANGE% *Set ORANGE = looks like this* %ENDCOLOR% 
      * %RED% *Set RED = looks like this* %ENDCOLOR% 
      * %PINK% *Set PINK = looks like this* %ENDCOLOR% 
      * %PURPLE% *Set PURPLE = looks like this* %ENDCOLOR% 
      * %TEAL% *Set TEAL = looks like this* %ENDCOLOR% 
      * %NAVY% *Set NAVY = looks like this* %ENDCOLOR% 
      * %BLUE% *Set BLUE = looks like this* %ENDCOLOR% 
      * %AQUA% *Set AQUA = looks like this* %ENDCOLOR% 
      * %LIME% *Set LIME = looks like this* %ENDCOLOR% 
      * %GREEN% *Set GREEN = looks like this* %ENDCOLOR% 
      * %OLIVE% *Set OLIVE = looks like this* %ENDCOLOR% 
      * %MAROON% *Set MAROON = looks like this* %ENDCOLOR% 
      * %BROWN% *Set BROWN = looks like this* %ENDCOLOR% 
      * %BLACK% *Set BLACK = looks like this* %ENDCOLOR% 
      * %GRAY% *Set GRAY = looks like this* %ENDCOLOR% 
      * %SILVER% *Set SILVER = looks like this* %ENDCOLOR% 
      * <span style="background: #808080 none repeat scroll 0% 0%; -moz-background-clip: -moz-initial; -moz-background-origin: -moz-initial; -moz-background-inline-policy: -moz-initial">%WHITE% *Set WHITE = looks like this (with gray background)* %ENDCOLOR%</span> 
      * The following color settings are enclosed in verbatim tags to avoid incorrect nesting of XHTML tags: <verbatim>
      * Set YELLOW = <font color="#ffff00">

</verbatim>

      * Set I = <img src="%ICONURLPATH{tip}%" alt="IDEA!" title="IDEA!" width="16" height="16" border="0" />    
      * Set M = <img src="%ICONURLPATH{arrowright}%" alt="MOVED TO..." title="MOVED TO..." width="16" height="16" border="0" />    
      * Set N = <img src="%ICONURLPATH{new}%" alt="NEW" title="NEW" width="30" height="16" border="0" />    
      * Set P = <img src="%ICONURLPATH{pencil}%" alt="REFACTOR" title="REFACTOR" width="16" height="16" border="0" />    
      * Set Q = <img src="%ICONURLPATH{help}%" alt="QUESTION?" title="QUESTION?" width="16" height="16" border="0" />

---++ Access Control Settings

   * Users or groups allowed to change or rename this %TOPIC% topic: 
      * Set ALLOWTOPICCHANGE = %MAINWEB%.TWikiAdminGroup
      * Set ALLOWTOPICRENAME = %MAINWEB%.TWikiAdminGroup    

---++ Creating New Preference Variables

You can introduce new VARIABLES and use them in your topics and templates. There is no need to change the TWiki engine (Perl scripts).
   * A preference is defined in a TWikiShorthand bullet item: ==[3 spaces] * [space] Set NAME = value== <br /> Example (as a nested bullet item, indented 6 spaces): 
      * Set WEBBGCOLOR = #FFFFC0    
   * Preferences are used as %TWIKIWEB%.TWikiVariables by enclosing the name in percent signs: ==%==. Example: 
      * When you write variable ==%WEBBGCOLOR%==, it gets expanded to =%WEBBGCOLOR%= . 

   * %X% The sequential order of the preference settings is significant. Define preferences that use other preferences FIRST. For example, set ==WEBCOPYRIGHT== before ==WIKIWEBMASTER== since the copyright notice uses the TWiki administrator e-mail address. 
   * %X% In order to protect your custom variables from being overwritten when upgrading the [[%TWIKIWEB%.%TOPIC%]] topic, it is recommended that custom variables are defined in [[%MAINWEB%.%TOPIC%]].

---++ Content Management Project

   * Boolean Variables
      * Set TRUE             = 1
      * Set FALSE            = 0
      * Set UNDEF            = 0
      * Set YES              = 1
      * Set NO               = 0
      * Set IN_PROGRESS      = 2
      
   * Boolean Variables used for the Review Process
      * Set INCLUDE_REVIEW = %NO%
      * Set INCLUDE_TEST   = %NO%
      * Set REVIEW_READY   = %NO%
      * Set TEST_READY     = %NO%
      * Set RELEASE_READY  = %NO%
      * Set REVIEW_PASSED  = %NO%
      * Set TEST_PASSED    = %NO%
      
   * Image Style
      * Set IMG_STYLE                  = margin: 10px 0px 10px 40px; padding: 6px; border: 1px solid #777; background: #BBB;

   * A decent Table Format
      * Set CM_TABLE_FORMAT            = %TABLE{ cellpadding="5,2,5,2" cellspacing="0" databg="#FFFFFF" headerbg="#8D929A" valign="middle" databg="#FFFFFF,#DDDDDD" tablewidth="100%" }%
   
   * Format for the Review Table
      * Set REV_TABLE_FORMAT           = %TABLE{ cellpadding="5,2,5,2" cellspacing="0" databg="#FFFFFF" headerbg="#8D929A" valign="middle" databg="#FFFFFF,#DDDDDD" tablewidth="100%" }%

   * Format for the Comment Table
      * Set COMMENT_TABLE_FORMAT       = %TABLE{ cellpadding="5,2,5,2" cellspacing="0" databg="#FFFFFF" headerbg="#8D929A" valign="middle" databg="#FFFFFF,#DDDDDD" tablewidth="100%" columnwidths="30,395,335,95,155" }%
      * Set COMMENT_TABLE_SHORT_FORMAT = %TABLE{ cellpadding="5,2,5,2" cellspacing="0" databg="#FFFFFF" headerbg="#8D929A" valign="middle" databg="#FFFFFF,#DDDDDD" tablewidth="100%" columnwidths="30,395,335,95,155" }%

   * FOrmat for the TAG Table
      * Set TAG_TABLE_FORMAT           = %TABLE{ cellpadding="5,2,5,2" cellspacing="0" databg="#FFFFFF" headerbg="#8D929A" valign="middle" databg="#FFFFFF,#DDDDDD" tablewidth="100%" columnwidths="30,395,335,95,155" }%    

   * Format for the Document Status Table
      * Set DOC_STATUS_TABLE_FORMAT    = %TABLE{ cellpadding="5,2,5,2" cellspacing="0" databg="#FFFFFF" headerbg="#8D929A" valign="middle" databg="#FFFFFF,#DDDDDD" caption="Document Status"}%

   * Format for the Review Status Table
      * Set REVIEW_STATUS_TABLE_FORMAT = %TABLE{ cellpadding="5,2,5,2" cellspacing="0" databg="#FFFFFF" headerbg="#8D929A" valign="middle" databg="#FFFFFF,#DDDDDD" caption="Review Status"}%
 
   * Bar Chart utilizing the Google Chart API
      * Set BARCHART                   = <img src="%REV_CH_BAR_PREFIX%%REV_PASSED%%7c%REV_TOTAL%"/>
      * Set BARCHART_S                 = <img src=\"%REV_CH_BAR_PREFIX_S%%REV_PASSED_S%%7c%REV_TOTAL_S%\"/>
      
   * Pie Chart utilizing the Google Chart API
      * Set PIECHART                   = <img src="%REV_CH_PIE_PREFIX%%REV_PASSED%,%REV_LEFT%"/>
      * Set PIECHART_S                 = <img alt=\"%REV_PASSED_S%\" src=\"%REV_CH_PIE_PREFIX_S%%REV_PASSED_S%,%REV_LEFT_S%\"/>
   
<!-- COMMENT OUT TABLES that should not be drawn on the Preferences Page

   * Define the document status table
      * Set SHOW_DOC_STATUS_TABLE        = %SHOW_DOC_STATUS_TABLE_11%%SHOW_DOC_STATUS_TABLE_10%%SHOW_DOC_STATUS_TABLE_01%%SHOW_DOC_STATUS_TABLE_00%
      * Set SHOW_DOC_STATUS_TABLE_SMALL  = %SHOW_DOC_STATUS_TABLE_SMALL_11%%SHOW_DOC_STATUS_TABLE_SMALL_10%%SHOW_DOC_STATUS_TABLE_SMALL_01%%SHOW_DOC_STATUS_TABLE_SMALL_00%
      * Set DOC_STATUS_TABLE             = %IF{"%RELEASE_READY%='%YES%'" else="$percntSHOW_DOC_STATUS_TABLE$percnt" then="$percntSHOW_DOC_STATUS_TABLE_SMALL$percnt"}%

   * define the document status table for INCLUDE_REVIEW = YES and INCLUDE_TEST = YES
      * Set DOC_STATUS_TABLE_11          = <table id="document-status-table">\n<tbody>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="4" class="heading">%WEB%%BR%!%TOPIC%</td>\n<td colspan="1" class="heading       * Set QUERY_PATTERN_OWNER          = $percntIF{\"\'$pattern(.*Local\s+OWNER\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)\'!=\'\'\" then=\'[[%MAINWEB%/$pattern(.*Local\s+OWNER\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)][$pattern(.*Local\s+OWNER\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)]]\' else=\'\'}$percnt
      * Set QUERY_PATTERN_REVIEWER       = $percntIF{\"\'$pattern(.*Local\s+REVIEWER\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)\'!=\'\'\" then=\'[[%MAINWEB%/$pattern(.*Local\s+REVIEWER\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)][$pattern(.*Local\s+REVIEWER\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)]]\' else=\'\'}$percnt
      * Set QUERY_PATTERN_TESTER         = $percntIF{\"\'$pattern(.*Local\s+TESTER\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)\'!=\'\'\" then=\'[[%MAINWEB%/$pattern(.*Local\s+TESTER\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)][$pattern(.*Local\s+TESTER\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)]]\' else=\'\'}$percnt
      * Set QUERY_PATTERN_DOC_AREA       = $percntIF{\"\'$pattern(.*Local\s+DOC_AREA\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)\'!=\'\'\" then=\'[[$pattern(.*Local\s+DOC_AREA\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)]]\' else=\'\'}$percnt
      * Set QUERY_PATTERN_DOC_ROLE       = $percntIF{\"\'$pattern(.*Local\s+DOC_ROLE\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)\'!=\'\'\" then=\'[[$pattern(.*Local\s+DOC_ROLE\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)]]\' else=\'\'}$percnt
      * Set QUERY_PATTERN_DOC_TYPE       = $percntIF{\"\'$pattern(.*Local\s+DOC_TYPE\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)\'!=\'\'\" then=\'[[$pattern(.*Local\s+DOC_TYPE\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)]]\' else=\'\'}$percnt

      * Set QUERY_PATTERN_REVIEWER_STATUS = %STATUS_$pattern(.*Local\s+REVIEW_PASSED\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)%
      * Set QUERY_PATTERN_TESTER_STATUS   = %STATUS_$pattern(.*Local\s+TEST_PASSED\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)%

      * Set QUERY_PATTERN_REVIEWER_CC    = $percntIF{\"\'$pattern(.*Local\s+REVIEWER\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)\'!=\'\'\" then=\'<div class=\"%STATUS_TO_CSS_$pattern(.*Local\s+REVIEW_PASSED\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)%\">[[%MAINWEB%/$pattern(.*Local\s+REVIEWER\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)][$pattern(.*Local\s+REVIEWER\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)]]</div>\' else=\'\'}$percnt
      * Set QUERY_PATTERN_TESTER_CC      = $percntIF{\"\'$pattern(.*Local\s+TESTER\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)\'!=\'\'\" then=\'<div class=\"%STATUS_TO_CSS_$pattern(.*Local\s+TEST_PASSED\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)%\">[[%MAINWEB%/$pattern(.*Local\s+TESTER\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)][$pattern(.*Local\s+TESTER\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)]]</div>\' else=\'\'}$percnt

      * Set STATUS_TO_CSS_0              = no
      * Set STATUS_TO_CSS_1              = yes
      * Set STATUS_TO_CSS_2              = in-progress
      
      * Set STATUS_0                     = <div class="no">failed</div>
      * Set STATUS_1                     = <div class="yes">passed</div>
      * Set STATUS_2                     = <div class="in-progress">in progress</div>

      * Set QUERY_PATTERN_REVIEWER_OLD   = $pattern(.*Local\s+REVIEWER\s*=\s*(\S*?)\s*\n.*)

   * Define the search string that finds all documents
      * Set QUERY_ALL                    = search="^*" scope="topic" web="%SearchWeb%" excludetopic="%ExcludeTopic%" regex="on" nosearch="on" nototal="on" header="%QUERY_OPTS_HEADER%" format="%QUERY_OPTS_FORMAT%"

   * Define the search string to find all documents where %%NOP%OWNER% left a comment

      * Set HELP_GRID_PROXY_INFO       = %TWISTY{showlink="grid-proxy-info" hidelink="Hide help page" start="hide" remember="on"}%\n<pre class="file">\n \nSyntax: grid-proxy-info [-help][-f proxyfile][-subject][...][-e [-h H][-b B]]\n \n    Options\n    -help, -usage             Displays usage\n    -version                  Displays version\n    -debug                    Displays debugging output\n    -file &lt;proxyfile&gt;  (-f)   Non-standard location of proxy\n    [printoptions]            Prints information about proxy\n    -exists [options]  (-e)   Returns 0 if valid proxy exists, 1 otherwise\n    \n    [printoptions]\n        -subject       (-s)   Distinguished name (DN) of subject\n        -issuer        (-i)   DN of issuer (certificate signer)\n        -identity             DN of the identity represented by the proxy\n        -type                 Type of proxy (full or limited)\n        -timeleft             Time (in seconds) until proxy expires\n        -strength             Key size (in bits)\n        -all                  All above options in a human readable format\n        -text                 All of the certificate\n        -path                 Pathname of proxy file\n \n    [options to -exists]      (if none are given, H = B = 0 are assumed)\n        -valid H:M     (-v)   time requirement for proxy to be valid\n        -hours H       (-h)   time requirement for proxy to be valid\n                              (deprecated, use -valid instead)\n        -bits  B       (-b)   strength requirement for proxy to be valid\n \n</pre>%ENDTWISTY%
      * Set HELP_GRID_PROXY_INIT       = %TWISTY{showlink="grid-proxy-init" hidelink="Hide help page" start="hide" remember="on"}%\n<pre class="file">\n \nSyntax: grid-proxy-init [-help][-pwstdin][-limited][-valid H:M] ...\n \n    Options\n    -help, -usage             Displays usage\n    -version                  Displays version\n    -debug                    Enables extra debug output\n    -q                        Quiet mode, minimal output\n    -verify                   Verifies certificate to make proxy for\n    -pwstdin                  Allows passphrase from stdin\n    -limited                  Creates a limited proxy\n    -independent              Creates a independent proxy\n    -old                      Creates a legacy globus proxy\n    -rfc                      Creates a RFC 3820 compliant proxy\n    -valid &lt;h:m&gt;              Proxy is valid for h hours and m \n                              minutes (default:12:00)\n    -hours &lt;hours&gt;            Deprecated support of hours option\n    -bits  &lt;bits&gt;             Number of bits in key {512|1024|2048|4096}\n    -policy &lt;policyfile&gt;      File containing policy to store in the\n                              ProxyCertInfo extension\n    -pl &lt;oid&gt;,                OID string for the policy language\n    -policy-language &lt;oid&gt;    used in the policy file\n    -path-length &lt;l&gt;          Allow a chain of at most l proxies to be \n                              generated from this one\n    -cert     &lt;certfile&gt;      Non-standard location of user certificate\n    -key      &lt;keyfile&gt;       Non-standard location of user key\n    -certdir  &lt;certdir&gt;       Non-standard location of trusted cert dir\n    -out      &lt;proxyfile&gt;     Non-standard location of new proxy cert\n \n</pre>%ENDTWISTY%      
      * Set HELP_GLOBUSRUN             = %TWISTY{showlink="globusrun" hidelink="Hide help page" start="hide" remember="on"}%\n<pre class="file">\n \nSyntax: globusrun [options] [RSL String]\n        globusrun -version[s]\n        globusrun -help\n \n    Options\n    -help | -usage\n           Display help\n    -version\n           Display version\n    -versions\n           Display versions of all activated modules\n    -i | -interactive \n           Run globusrun in interactive mode (multirequests only)\n    -f &lt;rsl filename&gt; | -file &lt;rsl filename&gt; \n           Read RSL from the local file &lt;rsl filename&gt;. The RSL can\n           be either a single job request, or a multirequest\n    -q | -quiet\n           Quiet mode (do not print diagnostic messages)\n    -o | -output-enable\n           Use the GASS Server library to redirect standout output\n           and standard error to globusrun. Implies -quiet\n    -s | -server\n           $(GLOBUSRUN_GASS_URL) can be used to access files local\n           to the submission machine via GASS. Implies -output-enable\n           and -quiet\n    -w | -write-allow\n           Enable the GASS Server library and allow writing to\n           GASS URLs. Implies -server and -quiet.\n    -mpirun &lt;integer&gt;\n           Currently a no-op.\n    -r &lt;resource manager&gt; | -resource  &lt;resource manager&gt; \n           Submit the RSL job request to the specified resource manager.\n           A resource manager can be specified in the following ways: \n \n           host\n           host:port\n           host:port/service\n           host/service\n           host:/service\n           host::subject\n           host:port:subject\n           host/service:subject\n           host:/service:subject\n           host:port/service:subject\n \n           For those resource manager contacts which omit the port, \n           service or subject field the following defaults are used:\n \n           port = 2119 \n           service = jobmanager \n           subject = subject based on hostname\n \n           This is a required argument when submitting a single RSL\n           request\n    -n | -no-interrupt\n           Cause SIGINT to terminate globusrun, while leaving the\n           submitted job to run to completion. By default the SIGINT\n           signal will be trapped and the job will be terminated\n    -k | -kill &lt;job ID&gt;\n           Kill a disconnected globusrun job\n    -status &lt;job ID&gt;\n           Print the current status of the specified job.\n    -b | -batch\n           Cause globusrun to terminate after the job is successfully\n           submitted to the scheduler. Useful for batch jobs. This option\n           cannot be used together with -interactive, and is also\n           incompatible with multi-request jobs.\n           If used with -s, files may be staged in to the job, but stdout\n           and stderr will not be redirected.\n           The "handle" or job ID of the submitted job will be written on\n           stdout.\n    -F | -fast-batch\n           Similar to -b but will exit as soon as the job has been sent\n           to the GRAM job manager service without waiting for a callback\n           with job submission state. Useful for hosts which are not able\n           to receive job state callbacks.\n    -refresh-proxy | -y &lt;job ID&gt;\n           Cause globusrun to delegate a new proxy to the job named by the\n           &lt;job ID&gt;\n    -stop-manager &lt;job  ID&gt;\n           Cause globusrun to stop the job manager, without killing the\n           job. If the save_state RSL attribute is present, then a\n           job manager can be restarted by using the restart RSL attribute.\n \n    Diagnostic Options\n    -p | -parse\n           Parse and validate the RSL only. Do not submit the job to\n           a GRAM gatekeeper\n    -a | -authenticate-only\n           Submit a gatekeeper "ping" request only. Do not parse the\n           RSL or submit the job request. Requires the -resource-manger \n           argument\n    -d | -dryrun\n           Submit the RSL to the job manager as a "dryrun" test\n           The request will be parsed and authenticated. The job manager\n           will execute all of the preliminary operations, and stop\n           just before the job request would be executed\n \n</pre>%ENDTWISTY%    
      * Set HELP_GLOBUS_URL_COPY       = %TWISTY{showlink="globus-url-copy" hidelink="Hide help page" start="hide" remember="on"}%\n<pre class="file">\n \nglobus-url-copy [options] &lt;sourceURL&gt; &lt;destURL&gt;\nglobus-url-copy [options] -f &lt;filename&gt;\n \n&lt;sourceURL&gt; may contain wildcard characters * ? and [ ] character ranges\nin the filename only.\nAny url specifying a directory must end with a forward slash '/'\n \nIf &lt;sourceURL&gt; is a directory, all files within that directory will\nbe copied.\n&lt;destURL&gt; must be a directory if multiple files are being copied.\n \nNote:  If the ftp server from the source url does not support the MLSD\n       command, this client will attempt to transfer subdirectories as\n       files, resulting in an error.  Recursion is not possible in this\n       case, but you can use the -c (continue on errors) option in order\n       to transfer the regular files from the top level directory.\n       **GridFTP servers prior to version 1.17 (Globus Toolkit 3.2)\n         do not support MLSD.\n \nOPTIONS\n  -help | -usage\n       Print help\n  -version\n       Print the version of this program\n  -versions\n       Print the versions of all modules that this program uses\n  -c | -continue-on-error\n       Do not die after any errors.  By default, program will exit after\n       most errors.\n  -a | -ascii\n       Convert the file to/from ASCII format to/from local file format\n  -b | -binary\n       Do not apply any conversion to the files. *default*\n  -f &lt;filename&gt;\n       Read a list of url pairs from filename.  Each line should contain\n       &lt;sourceURL&gt; &lt;destURL&gt;\n       Enclose URLs with spaces in double qoutes (").\n       Blank lines and lines beginning with # will be ignored.\n  -cd | -create-dest\n       Create destination directory if needed\n  -r | -recurse\n       Copy files in subdirectories\n  -fast\n       Recommended when using GridFTP servers. Use MODE E for all data\n       transfers, including reusing data channels between list and transfer\n       operations.\n  -q | -quiet \n       Suppress all output for successful operation\n  -v | -verbose \n       Display urls being transferred\n  -vb | -verbose-perf \n       During the transfer, display the number of bytes transferred\n       and the transfer rate per second.  Show urls being transferred\n  -dbg | -debugftp \n       Debug ftp connections.  Prints control channel communication\n       to stderr\n  -rst | -restart \n       Restart failed ftp operations.\n  -rst-retries &lt;retries&gt;\n       The maximum number of times to retry the operation before giving\n       up on the transfer.  Use 0 for infinite.  Default is 5.\n  -rst-interval &lt;seconds&gt;\n       The interval in seconds to wait after a failure before retrying\n       the transfer.  Use 0 for an exponential backoff.  Default is 0.\n  -rst-timeout &lt;seconds&gt;\n       Maximum time after a failure to keep retrying.  Use 0 for no\n       timeout.  Default is 0.\n  -rp | -relative-paths\n      The path portion of ftp urls will be interpereted as relative to the\n      user's starting directory on the server.  By default, all paths are\n      root-relative.  When this flag is set, the path portion of the ftp url\n      must start with %2F if it designates a root-relative path.\n  -s  &lt;subject&gt; | -subject &lt;subject&gt;\n       Use this subject to match with both the source and dest servers\n  -ss &lt;subject&gt; | -source-subject &lt;subject&gt;\n       Use this subject to match with the source server\n  -ds &lt;subject&gt; | -dest-subject &lt;subject&gt;\n       Use this subject to match with the destionation server\n  -tcp-bs &lt;size&gt; | -tcp-buffer-size &lt;size&gt;\n       specify the size (in bytes) of the buffer to be used by the\n       underlying ftp data channels\n  -bs &lt;block size&gt; | -block-size &lt;block size&gt;\n       specify the size (in bytes) of the buffer to be used by the\n       underlying transfer methods\n  -p &lt;parallelism&gt; | -parallel &lt;parallelism&gt;\n       specify the number of parallel data connections should be used.\n  -notpt | -no-third-party-transfers\n       turn third-party transfers off (on by default)\n  -nodcau | -no-data-channel-authentication\n       turn off data channel authentication for ftp transfers\n  -dcsafe | -data-channel-safe\n       set data channel protection mode to SAFE\n  -dcpriv | -data-channel-private\n       set data channel protection mode to PRIVATE\n  -off | -partial-offset\n       offset for partial ftp file transfers, defaults to 0\n  -len | -partial-length\n       length for partial ftp file transfers, used only for the source url,\n       defaults the full file.\n  -stripe\n       enable striped transfers on supported servers\n  -striped-block-size | -sbs\n       set layout mode and blocksize for striped transfers\n       If not set, server defaults will be used.\n       If set to 0, Partitioned mode will be used.\n       If set to &gt;0, Blocked mode will be used, with this as the blocksize.\n  -ipv6\n       use ipv6 when available (EXPERIMENTAL)\n  -nogridftp2\n       do not use GridFTP2 even when available\n \n</pre>%ENDTWISTY%
      * Set HELP_GLOBUS_JOB_RUN        = %TWISTY{showlink="globus-job-run" hidelink="Hide help page" start="hide" remember="on"}%\n<pre class="file">\n \nUsage: globus-job-run\n      [-help|-usage]                     print usage and exit\n      [-version]                         print version and exit\nUsage: globus-job-run\n      [-dumprsl]                         output RSL, don't run job\n      [-dryrun]                          verify RSL, don't run job\n      [-verify]                          perform dryrun, then run job\n      [-file             file]           read rest of arguments from file\n      [-stdin    [-l|-s] file]           global input default\n      [-stdout   [-l|-s] file]           global output default\n      [-stderr   [-l|-s] file]           global error output default\n      [-env              name=value]...  global environment default\n      [-args             [jobarg]...]    job-wide arguments\n      [ host-clause  |                   job description\n        -: host-clause...]               subjob description (multi-req)\n \nhost-clause syntax:\n      { contact string                   only the hostname is required.\n        [-np             N]              number of processing elements\n        [-count          N]              same as -np\n        [-host-count     nodes]          number of SMP nodes (IBM SP)\n        [-m[axtime]      minutes]        time to allocate for the job\n        [-p[roject]      projectID]      scheduling/accounting project ID\n        [-q[ueue]        queueID]        scheduling/accounting queue ID\n        [-d[ir]          directory]      working directory\n        [-env            name=value]...  environment binding\n        [-stdin  [-l|-s] file]           input\n        [-stdout [-l|-s] file]           output\n        [-stderr [-l|-s] file]           error output\n        [-x rsl-clause]                  RSL extension capability\n        [-l|-s] executable [args...]     executable and clause arguments\n \n   Job stdin defaults to /dev/null.\n   Job stdout/stderr default to stdout/stdout of globus-job-run.\n \n   The file modifiers -l and -s specify different filespaces:\n      -l[ocal]  file is relative to working directory of job      (DEFAULT)\n      -s[tage]  file relative to job request is staged to job host\n \n   The working directory of the submitted job defaults to $HOME.\n \n   Valid forms of the contact string are:\n       hostname\n       hostname:port\n       hostname:port/service\n       hostname/service\n       hostname:/service\n       hostname::subject\n       hostname:port:subject\n       hostname/service:subject\n       hostname:/service:subject\n       hostname:port/service:subject\n \n   More than one host-clause can be specified, in which case the job runs\n   on all of the hosts simultaneously.\n \n   The host clause begins with '-:' for a multi-request, and the contact string\n   of the remote resource for a single request. It allows any of the\n   specified options in any order. The first unrecognized (non-flagged)\n   term  is treated as the executable, with arguments following immediately\n   after.\n \n   In the multi-request case, arguments may be specified specifically for\n   each host-clause by appending them after the name of the executable, or\n   job-wide with the -args flag. In either case, arguments continue until\n   the end of the command-line or until the next '-:' flag signifying\n   a new host-clause.\n \n   Two '-:' flags in a row are interpreted as an escaped '-:' and the host-\n   clause continues until the next unpaired '-:' flag or end of input.\n \n   If more than one setting is defined (such as two -stdin definitions),\n   the setting defined last on the command line will be used.\n \n</pre>%ENDTWISTY%
      * Set HELP_GLOBUSRUN_WS          = %TWISTY{showlink="globusrun-ws" hidelink="Hide help page" start="hide" remember="on"}%\n<pre class="file">\n \nglobusrun-ws -help | -version[s]\nglobusrun-ws -usage [-validate | -submit | -monitor | -status | -kill]\n  Use the above to see which of the following are valid with each mode.\n \nModes of operation: (one should appear first on command line)\n -validate:\n       checks the job description for syntax errors and a subset\n       of semantic errors without making any service requests.\n -submit:\n       submits (or resubmits) a job to a job host in one of\n       three output modes: batch, interactive, or interactive-streaming.\n -monitor:\n       attaches to an existing job in interactive or\n       interactive-streaming output modes.\n -status:\n       reports the current state of the job and exits.\n -kill:\n       requests the immediate cancellation of the job and exits.\n \nOptions:\n -F, -factory &lt;contact&gt;:\n       If supplied, this option causes an EPR to be constructed using\n       ad-hoc methods that depend on GT implementation details.\n       For interoperability to other implementations of WS_GRAM,\n       the -factory-epr-file option should be used instead.\n      *format: [protocol://]{hostname|hostaddr}[:port][/service]\n      *default: https://localhost:8443/wsrf/services/ManagedJobFactoryService\n -Ft, -factory-type &lt;type&gt;:\n       in the absence of -factory-epr-file, this specifies a\n       type of scheduler.\n      *default: 'Fork' for single jobs and 'Multi' for multijobs\n -Ff, -factory-epr-file &lt;filename&gt;:\n       causes the EPR for the ManagedJobFactory to be read from the given\n       file. This EPR is used as the service endpoint for submission of the\n       job.\n -f, -job-description-file &lt;filename&gt;:\n       causes the job description to be read from the given file.\n       This description is modified according to the other options and\n       passed in the WS_GRAM submission messages.\n -c, -job-command [--] &lt;program&gt; [arg ...]:\n       takes all remaining globusrun-ws arguments as its arguments;\n       therefore it must appear last among globusrun-ws options. This\n       option causes globusrun-ws to generate a simple job description with\n       the named program and arguments.\n -o, -job-epr-output-file &lt;filename&gt;:\n       the created ManagedJob EPR will be written to the given\n       file following successful submission. The file will not be written\n       if the submission fails.\n -j, -job-epr-file &lt;filename&gt;:\n       causes the EPR for the ManagedJob to be read from the given file.\n       This EPR is used as the endpoint for service requests.\n -s, -streaming:\n       The standard output and standard error files of the job are\n       monitored and data is written to the corresponding output of\n       globusrun-ws. The standard output will contain ONLY job output data,\n       while the standard error may be a mixture of job error output as\n       well as globusrun-ws messages, unless -quiet is specified.\n      *implies: -staging-delegate if job description does not already\n       contain stdout and stderr endpoints\n      *note: use of -streaming (with or without -batch) places a hold state\n       on the job before cleanup.  you must let the job complete\n       or come back to it with -monitor or -kill\n -so, -stdout-file &lt;filename&gt;:\n       append stdout out stream to the specified file instead of to stdout.\n -se, -stderr-file &lt;filename&gt;:\n       append stderr out stream to the specified file instead of to stderr.\n -I, -submission-id &lt;uuid&gt;:\n       causes the job to be (re)submitted using the given uuid in the\n       reliability protocol.\n -If, -submission-id-file &lt;filename&gt;:\n       causes the uuid to be read from the given file. It is an error\n       to use with -submission-id\n -Io, -submission-id-output-file &lt;filename&gt;:\n       the uuid in use is written to the given file, whether this uuid\n       was generated for the user or given by one of the above\n       input options.\n -J, -job-delegate:\n       If supplied AND the job description does not already provide a\n       jobCredential element, globusrun-ws will delegate the\n       client credential to WS_GRAM and introduce the corresponding\n       element to the submission input.\n -S, -staging-delegate:\n       If supplied AND the job description does include staging or\n       cleanup directives AND the job description does not already provide\n       the necessary stagingCredential or transferCredential element(s),\n       globusrun-ws will delegate the client credential to WS_GRAM and RFT,\n       and introduce the corresponding elements to the submission input.\n -Jf, -job-credential-file &lt;filename&gt;:\n       If supplied AND the job description does not already provide a\n       jobCredential element, globusrun-ws will copy the supplied epr into\n       the job description.  This should be an epr returned from the\n       DelegationFactoryService intended for use by the job (or, in the\n       case of a multijob, for authenticating to the subjobs).\n      *note: for multijob descriptions, only the top level jobCredential\n       will be copied into.\n -Sf, -staging-credential-file &lt;filename&gt;:\n       If supplied AND the job description does not already provide a\n       stagingCredential element, globusrun-ws will copy the supplied epr\n       into the job description.  This should be an epr returned from the\n       DelegationFactoryService intended for use with the RFT service\n       associated with the ManagedJobService.\n      *note: this option is ignored for multijobs.\n -Tf, -transfer-credential-file &lt;filename&gt;:\n       If supplied, globusrun-ws will copy the epr into each of the\n       stage in, stage out, and cleanup elements that do not already\n       contain a transferCredential element.  This should be an epr\n       returned from the DelegationFactoryService intended for use by\n       RFT to authenticate with the target gridftp server.\n      *note: this option is ignored for multijobs.\n -b, -batch:\n       enables batch mode. the tool prints the resulting ManagedJob EPR as\n       the sole standard output (unless in quiet mode) and exits.\n      *note: without this, -submit is equivalent to\n       -submit -batch immediately followed by -monitor.\n -q, -quiet:\n       all non-fatal status and protocol-related messages are suppressed.\n -n, -no-cleanup:\n       the default behavior of trapping interrupts (SIGINT) and canceling\n       the job is disabled. Instead, the interrupt simply causes the tool\n       to exit without affecting the ManagedJob resource.\n -host, -host-authz:\n       The GSI 'host authorization' rule is used to verify that the\n       service is using a host credential appropriate for the underlying\n       service address information.\n      *default\n -self, -self-authz:\n       The GSI 'self authorization' rule is used to verify that the\n       service is using a (proxy) credential derived from the same\n       identity as the client's.\n -subject, -subject-authz &lt;subject name&gt;:\n       The service must be using a credential with the exact subject\n       name provided by this option.\n -p, -private:\n       If supplied, privacy-protection is enabled between globusrun-ws\n       and WS_GRAM or GridFTP services. It is a fatal error to select\n       privacy protection if it is not available due to build options or\n       other security settings.\n      *note: currently only works with https endpoints\n -T, -http-timeout &lt;milliseconds&gt;:\n       Set timeout for HTTP socket, in milliseconds, for all Web services\n       interactions.\n      *default: 120000 (2 minutes).\n -term, -termination +&lt;HH:MM&gt;|&lt;mm/dd/yyyy HH:MM&gt;:\n       Set a termination time (+relative to now).\n      *default: +24:00\n -dbg, -debug:\n       Display message and GridFTP debug output on stderr\n -pft, -print-fault-type:\n       When a fault occurs, display a line containing\n       Fault Type: fault-type\n       on stderr\n -ipv6, -allow-ipv6:\n       Allow streaming transfers to use IPV6.\n -passive:\n       Force streaming transfers to use MODE S to allow for passive mode\n       transfers. (Useful if you're behind a firewall, but expensive\n       because there is no connection caching).\n -nodcau:\n       Disable data channel authentication on streaming transfers.\n \n</pre>%ENDTWISTY%
      * Set HELP_VOMS_PROXY_INFO       = %TWISTY{showlink="voms-proxy-info" hidelink="Hide help page" start="hide" remember="on"}%\n<pre class="file">\n \nvoms-proxy-info: \n \nSyntax: voms-proxy-info [-help][-file proxyfile][-subject][...][-exists [-hours H][-bits B]]\n \n   Options\n   -help, -usage             Displays usage\n   -version                  Displays version\n   -debug                    Displays debugging output\n   -file &lt;proxyfile&gt; ---++ Related Topics

   * %WEBPREFSTOPIC% has preferences of the %WEB% web. 
   * %MAINWEB%.%WIKIUSERSTOPIC% has a list of user topics. User topics can have optional user preferences. 
   * %TWIKIWEB%.TWikiVariables has a list of common =%VARIABLES%=. 
   * %TWIKIWEB%.TWikiAccessControl explains how to restrict access by users or groups. 
   * TWiki:Plugins.PreferencesPlugin makes editing preferences a snap. 

__Note__: Can't edit? [[%SCRIPTURLPATH{"view"}%/%WEB%/%TOPIC%?raw=on][View raw topic]]

   * Set G = %ICON{choice-no}%    
   * Set O = %ICON{choice-cancel}%

   * Set TINYMCEPLUGIN_DISABLE = 1
